              <div class="Box-header f6 color-text-secondary"> <strong class="color-text-primary text-bold"> Rick-Anderson </strong> commented <relative-time datetime="2020-06-02T20:40:20Z" class="no-wrap">

              <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px"> 
               <p>Create an include (something like <code>https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/includes/reservedRouting.md</code></p> 
               <p>With the info from <a href="https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/wiki/MVC-Reserved-Keywords">https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/wiki/MVC-Reserved-Keywords</a> on routing. Be stronger, something like</p> 
               <p>These keywords should <em><strong>not</strong></em> be used for link generations, as model bound parameters, or top level properties.</p> 
               <p>Add the include to the 3</p>

               <h2>Problem</h2>

               <p>When I go to use it to query for many results the operations tell me nothing about what and why they will do. I only have types to work with.</p>

            <div class="flex-auto" style="width: 80%;"> 
             <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret"> 
              <div class="Box-header f6 color-text-secondary"> <strong class="color-text-primary text-bold"> g-savitha </strong> commented <relative-time datetime="2021-01-17T11:50:05Z" class="no-wrap">
                Jan 17, 2021
               </relative-time> 
              </div> 
              <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px"> 
               <p>Currently, few icons are not visible in dark theme. Make them visible by using theme neutral icons. May be we can make use of <a href="https://shields.io/" rel="nofollow">https://shields.io/</a> to generate our own kind of badges. For eg: <a href="https://img.shields.io/badge/-JavaScript-333333?style=flat&amp;logo=javascript" rel="nofollow">Javascript</a>.</p>

             <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret"> 
              <div class="Box-header f6 color-text-secondary"> <strong class="color-text-primary text-bold"> Elfo404 </strong> commented <relative-time datetime="2021-06-02T11:20:56Z" class="no-wrap">
                Jun 2, 2021
               </relative-time> 
              </div> 
              <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px"> 
               <p>Multiple Explore-related components still make use of <code>GrafanaTheme</code>.<br> Since Grafana 8.0 introduces <code>GrafanaTheme2</code> and deprecates <code>GrafanaTheme</code> we should migrate to the new theme.</p> 
               <p>This should probably be done in multiple small PRs that target a small amount of components to make review easy.</p> 
               <p>Also the following data sources have components that need to be migrated:</p> 
               <ul class="contains-task-list"> 
                <li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled class="task-list-item-checkbox"> Elasticsearch</li> 
                <li></li> 
               </ul>

           <div class="flex-auto"> 
            <h1 class="f2-light color-text-primary lh-condensed mt-1 mb-2"> <a data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;explore.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;click_context&quot;:&quot;MARKETPLACE_APP_CARD&quot;,&quot;click_target&quot;:&quot;MARKETPLACE_APP&quot;,&quot;click_visual_representation&quot;:&quot;MARKETPLACE_APP_TITLE&quot;,&quot;actor_id&quot;:null,&quot;record_id&quot;:1110,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/explore&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="0404e579f4cb84652ca23d39f2af2a62ce11ec4f7db739905fbde94774b2cdc8" data-ga-click="Explore, go to marketplace app, location:explore feed; text:Stale" href="/marketplace/stale" data-view-component="true"> Stale </a> </h1> 
            <div class="markdown-body f5 color-text-secondary mb-2"> 
             <p>Automatically close stale Issues and Pull Requests that tend to accumulate during a project.</p> 
             <h2>How it works</h2> 
             <p>After a period of inactivity, a label will be applied to mark an issue as stale, and optionally post a comment to notify contributors that the Issue or Pull Request will be closed.</p> 
             <p>If the Issue or Pull Request is updated, or anyone comments, then the stale label is removed.</p> 
             <p>If no more activity occurs, the Issue or Pull Request will be automatically closed with an optional comment.</p> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </article> 
       </div> <!--// Octoverse //-->
